Criminal Lawsuit Settlement - Request to Suspend Trial - Settlement Reached in Case of Deceiving in Foreign Socks - Court Approves Suspension of Trial 114

Dong Baosheng, the owner of Tongmao Silk Shop at No. 30, Pentang Lane, British Concession, had partnered with Feng Xingbo, Shen Xinzuan, and others to open Yichangxiang Grocery Store in Chunyuan Lane, Nine Acres, in the city, as a branch of Tongmao Silk Shop. Last month, he planned to establish Tongmao's second branch at Junfu Lane, Eight Immortals Bridge, French Concession, named Chengji National Goods Store, and hired Gu Xiwun, who was a foreign socks broker, as a purchasing agent. Gu had long-standing business relationships with sock factories in Datuan Town, Liuzao Town, Nanhui County, etc. After being hired, he purchased four to five thousand dozen foreign socks from various sock factories on behalf of Chengji, to prepare for Chengji's opening. The required price was paid in bank and money shop term bills, or promised to be paid in cash after the opening. Unexpectedly, when the factory owners Wang Yongting, Sun Yaojie, Ni Lechu, Zhou Bosheng, Shen Zhenmiao, Tang Yinlian, etc., came to Shanghai to collect the money, Chengji at Eight Immortals Bridge and Yichangxiang at Nine Acres had both closed. Dong, Feng, Shen, and others had all disappeared. Only then did the creditors realize that they had been deceived. They reported to the French Concession police station and requested an investigation. Later, they learned that Dong Baosheng was located at Tongmao Silk Shop. They went to negotiate, but found that Tongmao's interior was also empty. Therefore, they twisted Dong and went to the Old Gate police station. The police chief ordered an investigation to clarify that the location of the deception was not in the Public Concession. Then, the creditors twisted Dong and sent him to the Second District First Precinct of the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau, ordering him to provide a guarantor for bail. However, Dong initially pleaded ignorance. The creditors were all small businesses, deeply afraid that the money would be lost. They hired a lawyer to file a private prosecution against Dong Baosheng, Feng Xingbo, and Shen Xinzuan in the First Special District District Court for fraud, arguing that although the location of the crime was in the Chinese and French Concessions, the headquarters was in the Public Concession, and should be under the jurisdiction of your court. They requested that the case be summoned and punished in accordance with Article 339 of the Criminal Law, and attached a civil lawsuit, ordering the defendants to repay the plaintiffs' money, etc. After Dong and others were sued, they knew they could not escape punishment and asked someone to come forward and settle the matter. Yesterday afternoon was the date for the trial of the case. The plaintiff's lawyer stated in court that the case had now been settled and requested a suspension of the trial. Judge Huang Fu Yu approved it. Since the promulgation of the new Code of Criminal Procedure, such lawsuits, even if settled out of court, cannot be withdrawn, and applying for a suspension of the trial may also be a method of remedy.

Rickshaw Driver Beaten to Death by a Japanese Person - Autopsy Results - Determined to Have Died from a Fractured Skull - The Japanese Murderer Has Already Surrendered 115

Wang Deyuan, a native of Taizhou, 34 years old, made a living pulling rickshaws. At about 3:00 AM on the 3rd of this month, at the intersection of Zhapu Road and Bazilu, an altercation occurred with a Japanese person, Tsuruyama Tatsuya, over the rickshaw fare. He was then struck in the head and chest twice by the Japanese person, fell to the ground injured, and was taken to Tongren Hospital by the police who arrived at the scene. Medical treatment was ineffective and he died at 1:00 PM that afternoon. The Hongkou police station was notified and ordered detectives to investigate. Wang's body was taken to the Philander Road Mortuary to await the autopsy. The details have already been reported. The First Special District District Court appointed Prosecutor Guo Wei to visit the mortuary with forensic doctors to conduct the autopsy to clarify the truth. After the autopsy was completed, it was found that the deceased had a fractured skull and died from the injuries. It was also learned that the Japanese person had already surrendered to the Hongkou police station a few days ago, admitting that he had beaten the deceased at the time. He was then transferred by the police station to the Japanese consulate for detention. The deceased's family, through his sister Chen Wangshi, reported to the fellow villagers' association, which hired a lawyer on their behalf to handle all legal procedures. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Guo and others visited the mortuary again and informed the Western police chief of the police station and the deceased's family of the autopsy findings. It was then determined that the deceased Wang Deyuan, male, died from a fractured skull and injuries sustained before his death. The suspect, Japanese person Tsuruyama Tatsuya, should be prosecuted by the police station to the Japanese consular court. The body was handed over to his sister, Chen Wangshi, who signed a bond to take it back for burial.

Lu Xihou and Others - Another New Case Discovered - Accused of Embezzling 15,000 Yuan - Lu Zutong is Also One of the Victims 116

The China Industrial Bank closed down on the day after the Double Tenth Festival last year. Lu Xihou, the director in charge of the bank, manager Lu Mengxiang, and Sun Xiren were suspected by the police of embezzlement, fraud, and breach of trust. Now all civil matters have been resolved one by one, so Judge Qian Hongye of the criminal court continued the trial yesterday afternoon. The various embezzled amounts were only discovered after the accountants audited the bank's accounts. It was found that Lu Xihou, Lu Mengxiang, and Chen Zutong, the manager of the Kunshan branch of the bankrupt Ningbo Industrial Bank, colluded to embezzle a huge sum of 15,000 yuan from the China Industrial Bank. Therefore, the police have now added another case, and Lu Zutong has also been listed as a defendant. However, he failed to appear after being summoned. The Western detective in charge reported that after the police received and read the report made by the bank's liquidation accountants, they discovered that the bank issued three promissory notes on October 1 last year, each for 5,000 yuan, totaling 15,000 yuan, all due on October 11. Lu Zutong cashed out this item. It was found to be illegally obtained benefits, causing more losses to the bank's creditors, etc. He also presented the promissory note and related account books for inspection and verification. Judge Qian then questioned Xi, Meng, and the two defendants. He then ordered the police to prepare a written report on the investigation of the promissory note to make it easier to understand, and ordered the defendants to wait for another trial next Monday afternoon.

Evil Young Man Indirectly Causes Death - Sun Chasusn Sued and Detained 117

Shi Huieng, a native of Liyang, residing in the Hongkou Tilan Bridge area (a descendant of Shi Kefa, a great politician of the late Ming Dynasty), is a distinguished family in Liyang. She regretted it deeply and returned to Shanghai in shame. She secretly swallowed a gold ring, intending to commit suicide. Her husband noticed it and extended medical treatment to purge it. Unexpectedly, last month, Zhang Jinmei was seen again by Sun Xingxun when she returned to her hometown, and he threatened her again. He came to Shanghai in the same car and was taken to the local court by a Lu police officer. He was taken into custody pending trial. After Zhang Jinmei returned home from the court, she refused to eat or drink. Also, due to swallowing gold and drowning, her internal organs were damaged. Prosecutor Xiao filed a public prosecution. Yesterday morning, Judge Chen Jingyi specially opened the Ninth Court for trial. Shi Huigeng, represented by lawyer Hu Yuanjun, arrived in court, claiming to be a 37-year-old from Liyang, and also claimed that his wife Zhang Jinmei was deceived and died in shame, causing the plaintiff's family to be ruined. His reputation, money and spirit have suffered great damage. He requested a heavy investigation according to the law. After obtaining the supply of food, the interrogation officer stated that the judge handling the case was currently on leave, and he waited for the extension of the hearing. The defendant Sun Xingxun was also taken into custody.

Two Women Fight Over a Child Case - Chen Yipeizhen Appeals - Obstetrics Female Doctor Arrives at Court to Testify - Court Ordered to Summon Children to Court Pending Hearing 118

Chen Yipeizhen, a Beiping woman from outside the house of Chen Yide, a deceased local who operated real estate in Fa Zujie Beile Road No. 360, previously extended the lawyer's agent to file a case in the Civil Court of the Second Special Court against Chen Zhou, the wife of Chen, to confirm the birth son. It is said that in the twelfth year of the Republic of China, she married Chen as a concubine. In July of the fifteenth year, she gave birth to son Xiongguan, named Nengyi. Because she suffered from illness after childbirth, it was inconvenient to raise her. Chen brought back and handed it over to the big wife Chen Zhou to raise him. Xiongguan is ten years old this year. After Chen Yide's death, he wanted to return to him, but Chen Zhou refused to allow him to. He presented photos of his cohabitation with him and other children and He Cuizhen, an obstetrician who gave birth, as evidence. The defendant Chen Zhou claimed that the child was born to her and ordered the two to take the child to the Zhenru Forensic Research Institute for scientific identification of the blood of both parties and the child. As a result, it was believed that both parties had the possibility of giving birth to Nengyi. The court ruled that the ruling rejected the plaintiff's claim. Chen Yipeizhen refused to accept the ruling and filed an appeal with the Third Division of the Jiangsu Higher Court. According to the petition, the High Court was heard yesterday by President Guo Dezhang and by Yu Shiyi and Fan En. The two judges specially opened the Civil Three Court for trial. Both parties were represented by lawyers. First, Chen Yipeizhen, the appellant's representative lawyer, stated the reasons for the appeal, requesting that the original judgment be abolished and a new judgment be made, confirming that Chen Nengyi was the appellant's biological son. The original trial judgment held that the appellant failed to fulfill the duty of proof in the original trial, but the appellant had presented photos and obstetrician doctors as the only evidence. The other party made empty claims, denied the facts, and did not submit any reliable evidence. The original trial did not examine the evidence submitted by the original case in detail. The words in the appraisal certificate of the forensic research institute were ambiguous and a detailed examination is now requested. A diary ledger used by Chen Yide during his lifetime was also presented, with Chen's handwritten records of Nengyi's date and time of birth. Then the representative lawyer of the appellee defended the reasons stated by the appellant's lawyer. The court summoned witness He Cuizhen, an obstetrician, to the case. She first stated that she was introduced to me by Dr. Sun Jieqing, a friend of Chen Yide, to give birth. When she was about to give birth, Chen called me. The rest is the same as what was provided in the original trial. The court verified the words and instructed the lawyers of both parties to suspend the investigation of Chen Yide's handwriting during his lifetime in this case, and instructed the appellee's agent to submit the case next time. The appellee must also bring the child to the court for questioning next time. At the end of the hearing, the court adjourned.

A Discussion with Concession Health Authorities Regarding Malaria 119

Regarding the outbreak of malignant malaria in Minhang, South Shanghai, and the repeated warnings to travelers by the Municipal Council's Health Department, a recent report quoted a certain entomologist as saying that malarial mosquitoes are not good at flying and have never been seen flying more than a mile away. Therefore, this port will never be affected by the malarial mosquitoes of Minhang, and will not endanger the health of the Bodhisattva. Now, a certain person in charge of the Municipal Council's Health Department informed reporters of two points: Shanghai people do not necessarily have to wait for malaria mosquitoes to invade Shanghai to be infected with malaria. The invasion of malarial mosquitoes in Shanghai has nothing to do with whether the mosquitoes are good at flying. The reason why the Health Department has repeatedly warned is that tourists who go to Minhang are not adequately protected and contract malaria, bringing germs back to Shanghai. Second, tourists' cars often carry mosquitoes, in varying amounts. Even when driving from the countryside near Shanghai to the central area, they often carry one or two or three or four mosquitoes. Cars coming to Shanghai from Minhang, if not paying attention, can also be used by malaria mosquitoes as a means of transportation. It can be proved that people who have cars often find that mosquitoes are clustered in the car in the morning, so Shanghai is not completely safe and the importance of cooperation between tourists and health authorities is clear. As for malarial mosquitoes not being good at flying, they cannot fly more than 200 yards each time. This is not consistent with modern scientific discoveries and is not related to the original purpose of malaria prevention.

Representatives of the Vegetable Stalls on Father She Road Petitioned the Social Affairs Bureau Yesterday Morning 120

The vegetable stalls on Father She Road in the French Concession were repeatedly banned by the French Concession police station and moved to Kangti Road. Unexpectedly, they were still expelled. Due to livelihood relations, all the stallholders petitioned and negotiated with party and government agencies and the French Concession Chinese Ratepayers Association and the Citizens' Federation. All the vegetable vendors, since the ban, have been extremely panic-stricken about their livelihoods. Yu Tianbi, a staff member of the bureau's First Section, received them and replied that he had already submitted it to the municipal government for verification and urged the vegetable vendors to wait patiently for a solution. The vegetable vendors thought it was satisfactory before leaving. The petition stated: "We, the vegetable vendors, have been unreasonably banned from setting up stalls on Kangti Road by the French Concession authorities. We have already reported the circumstances and requested that the Bureau consider the livelihoods of the stallholders and provide relief. However, many days have passed and we have not been able to resume setting up stalls. It is difficult to obtain a joint letter from 51 stores on the road, requesting the French police station to report that Mr. Fervolet, the Inspector General of the French Police Department, replied in a letter in the 20th year of the Republic of China, approving the establishment of stalls, requesting that the ban be temporarily suspended on the premise of revitalizing the market. However, we have not received the permission of the police station, which has caused the lives of the 83 households and all the children in the family to be extremely panic-stricken. If this situation continues to be unresolved, we will all starve to death. Therefore, we have to continue to submit the petition. We urge you, the head of the court, to sympathize with the livelihoods of the peddlers and approve negotiations with the French authorities to find a way to restore the stalls in order to maintain people's livelihood. We cannot win the urgency of awaiting orders.

Dr. Zhang Jingduo Returns to China from Italy 123

Zhang Jingduo, a native of Gaoling County, Shaanxi, graduated from Wuchang Literary Middle School and Xi'an Theological Seminary. Later, he studied at Fu Jen Catholic University in Peiping for one year. In the autumn of the 20th year of the Republic of China, he went to Rome to study abroad. He studied at the Pontifical Faculty of Law for two years and obtained a doctorate in law. Then he went to Milan, Italy, to study philosophy at the Italian Catholic University registered by the government and obtained a doctorate in philosophy. He also graduated from the Graduate School of Education. Milan is a large commercial port in Italy. There are more than 300 overseas Chinese doing business there, with very few intellectual classes, so they are often looked down upon and bullied. Mr. Zhang, motivated by the righteousness of his compatriots, contacted them to unite and help each other. He also tried his best to promote the culture of his motherland, changing the attitude of the Italian people towards China. During the previous visits to Milan by industrial, educational, transportation, military and aviation observation groups to Europe, Mr. Zhang must have sincerely entertained and guided them. After years of studying abroad, due to the repeated natural disasters and banditry in his hometown, there was very little financial assistance. Fortunately, the remuneration of writing and lectures was used to supplement the expenses. His spirit of frugality and diligence in learning is enough to be a model for the academic community. Now, the Shanxi government has hired him to run social education undertakings, so he packed up and returned to China. He arrived in Shanghai on the Italian Wheel Kang Defante a few days ago. Mr. Zhang is only 30 years old, knows Chinese, English, French, Italian, German, Latin, and other languages, has profound knowledge, and is passionate about patriotism. He will be able to work steadily to develop the northwest.

Weng Longping Attacked and Wounded by a Revenger 132

Weng Longping, 31 years old, from Jiangsu Province, resides on the upper floor of the Tongxingtai stove shop at No. 24 Xinzha Road, where he has lived for years. Yesterday afternoon around 3:30 PM, the assailant Shen Xiaomao suddenly arrived, armed with a sharp blade, seeking revenge on Weng. When he encountered Weng, Shen, without asking any questions, raised his knife and stabbed Weng repeatedly all over his body. Weng was unable to avoid the attack and was stabbed six times—three times in his right leg and three times in his left arm. Blood gushed out like a fountain, and he collapsed. The assailant, seeing that his purpose was achieved, took the opportunity to escape without a trace. Nearby Chinese police officers sent Weng to Zhilong Hospital for treatment. As for why Weng was attacked by Shen, it is said that Shen had previously committed a crime and was wanted by the police, but his whereabouts were unknown. Weng revealed Shen's hiding place, and Shen was arrested by the police and convicted according to law. He was recently released after serving his term, so he came to seek revenge on Weng.

Sacrifice for a Gold Ring: Zhang Jiquan Hangs Himself Due to Inability to Pay 134

Zhang Jiquan, 41 years old, the head server at the Huiquan Bathhouse at No. 34, Lane 3, Xiaoyouli, Haig Road, Xujiahui, has worked there for over ten years. He is known for his honesty and is deeply trusted by the owner. On the afternoon of the 4th of this month, Xu Shunfa (also known as A Liuyou), who runs a fish shop in the town, went to Huiquan for a bath. Xu wrapped a gold ring and jade ring and a watch, and gave it to Zhang Jiquan for safekeeping. About an hour later, after Xu finished bathing and dressing, Zhang returned the original package to Xu, who did not open it to wear, but put it in his pocket. Xu first went to the Catholic Church to collect debts, then to the Yangjiaku storytelling theatre to listen to a play. Returning home around 10 PM, he discovered the watch and ring were missing. He rushed to the bathhouse to ask Zhang for them. Zhang replied that he had already returned the package and saw Xu put it in his pocket. Xu denied receiving them, accusing Zhang of swallowing it. He brought Shen Yuchu and Person A, and held Zhang, demanding that he return the original items. Shen and others mediated, and each side agreed to share half of the loss, with Zhang compensating Xu thirty yuan, to be paid on the 7th. Person A asked Zhang Jiquan for a reward of five yuan, of which three yuan was paid, with three yuan still owing, guaranteed by Shen Yutian. The night before last, Shen asked for the money, and an argument occurred because Zhang had no money (some say Shen slapped him twice). The thirty yuan due date was also approaching, so in a moment of desperation, Zhang committed suicide yesterday morning at 5 AM, secretly entering the kitchen shed of the Huiquan Bathhouse, and hanging himself. When discovered, he had already died. The body was reported to the local police station and transported to the Tongren Auxiliary Yuantang for examination. It is known that the deceased's family lives at No. 60 Xiaoyouli, leaving behind a wife, three sons, two daughters, and a daughter-in-law, a family of eight, all dependent on his income. The children are all minors, and their livelihood has been cut off, leaving them in a dire situation.

Report on the Conclusion of the Emergency Hospital for Epidemic Diseases: Dysentery Most Prevalent This Year 135

A total of over three thousand patients were diagnosed and hospitalized. The total number of deaths was seventeen. More than ten thousand patients were treated in the internal and external medicine departments.

The Emergency Hospital for Epidemic Diseases on North Xizang Road, which opened on July 7th of this year and closed on September 30th, has officially released a written report on its medical services. The following is a record:

Outpatient Diagnosis

Dysentery: 562 cases; Acute Enteritis: 483 cases; Influenza: 448 cases; Acute Gastroenteritis: 306 cases; Acute Gastritis: 126 cases; Malaria: 126 cases; Constipation: 77 cases; Indigestion: 20 cases; Trauma: 17 cases; Poisoning: 16 cases; Bronchitis: 16 cases; Heart Disease: 15 cases; Typhoid Fever: 14 cases; Ascariasis: 10 cases; Measles: 10 cases; Burns: 7 cases; Tonsillitis, Miscellaneous Ailments, and Stomach Ailments: 6 cases each; Intestinal Inflammation: 9 cases; Nephritis, Calcium Deficiency and Convulsions: 4 cases; Insomnia, Diphtheria, Beriberi, Acute Pneumonia, Hysteria: 3 cases each; Menstrual Irregularities, Stroke (Hemiplegia), and Tuberculosis: 2 cases each; Liver Abscess, Scarlet Fever, Cystitis, Rubella, Jaundice, Intestinal Tuberculosis, Peritonitis, Erysipelas, and Hemiplegia: 1 case each. Total: 2,410 cases.

Inpatient Diagnosis

Acute Gastroenteritis: 188 cases; Dysentery: 147 cases; Acute Enteritis: 57 cases; Acute Gastritis: 35 cases; Heatstroke, Typhoid Fever, and Malaria: 10 cases each; Miscellaneous Ailments: 3 cases; Acute Pneumonia and Relapsing Fever: 2 cases each; Heart Disease, Beriberi, Cellulitis, Epidemic Meningitis, and Peritonitis: 1 case each. Total: 469 cases.

Number of Deaths

Dysentery: 6 deaths; Acute Pneumonia, Acute Enteritis, and Typhoid Fever: 2 deaths each; Heart Disease, Heatstroke, Acute Gastroenteritis, Beriberi, and Peritonitis: 1 death each. Total: 17 deaths.

The hospital also reported the following numbers of patients treated in its internal and external medicine departments this year because they opened a separate outpatient clinic: Surgery: over 4,000 patients; Dermatology and Venereology: over 3,200 patients; Ophthalmology, Otolaryngology: over 2,600 patients; Internal Medicine: over 1,900 patients; Pediatrics: over 700 patients; Obstetrics: over 240 patients. Total: 12,581 patients.

Further Details on the Case of a Handgun Retrieved from Under the Xinzha Bridge 139

Third Section Interrogated the Parties Yesterday

The former residence of the late Qian Guisan, Director of the Zhabei Municipal Government, located at No. 63 Changan Road, Zhabei, discovered a handgun and bullets in a kerosene box while demolishing a mezzanine. Fearing an accident, Qian's female owner ordered her maid to sink the handgun under the Xinzha Bridge, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. It has been learned that the case originated when Li Guiqing, the deputy leader of the detective squad of the Xinzha Branch, received information that Qian's family was hiding a handgun and bullets. Therefore, Deputy Leader Li reported to Team Leader Bao Ziying, Deputy Team Leader Shi Zuhan, and Leader Liu Changpei, who reported to Director Liao of the branch, who dispatched police officer Sun Kezhi, Zhang Linqing, and detective Zang Nai to investigate. Qian Lu's explained that she had ordered her maid to sink the handgun under the Xinzha Bridge. Therefore, the police officers took Qian Lu's maid Zhang Chen's into custody. At the same time, the police officers hired a boat to retrieve the handgun and bullets. The handgun was found to be No. 2243, and there were twenty-nine bullets. They were taken to the branch, interrogated, and then released on bail. The handgun and bullets were sent to the Second Section of the Public Security Bureau. Yesterday morning, the Third Section used the telephone to instruct the Xinzha Branch to summon Qian Lu's and the maid Zhang Chen's for interrogation. The confessions were roughly as follows: Qian Lu's confessed, "My late husband, Qian Guisan, was in charge of the security forces for many years. We didn't know there was a handgun on the mezzanine. We only discovered a kerosene box while demolishing the mezzanine the other day. I was afraid it would harm someone, so I put it in a cloth bag and ordered the maid to sink it under the Xinzha Bridge to avoid future trouble. Unexpectedly, the Xinzha Branch found out, leading to the interrogation." The maid Zhang Chen's confessed, "I was ordered by my mistress to throw the handgun into the river." The rest of her statement was similar to Lu's. After reviewing the confessions, the interrogating officer released them.

Li Yuzao Files a Counterclaim

Dancer Ren Aina, accompanied by her mother Ren Dongshi, recently retained attorney Yin Shouguang to sue Li Yuzao in the Criminal Court of the District Court for enticing a woman under the age of twenty to leave her family. The defendant Li Yuzao did not appear but was represented by an attorney who filed a counterclaim, accusing the plaintiff, mother and daughter, of attempted fraud and of making false accusations. The judge asked why the defendant had repeatedly failed to appear and should provide a reason for his absence. The defendant's attorney presented several prescriptions, stating that the defendant was unable to appear due to illness. The judge then instructed that the defendant must appear at the next hearing to finalize the case and avoid further delays.

Student of Zhaohe Middle School Dies Tragically 143

Dai Hainan, a 17-year-old from Yixing who lived at No. 17 Gengyuli, Bobert Road, French Concession, and studied at Zhaohe Middle School in Shanghai, was walking on the Bund outside the French Concession on the afternoon of the 5th of this month at around 6:00 PM. Tram No. 16 of the French Electric Company, Route 10, was heading from Lujiawan to the Bund and turning east towards the south when it collided with a cargo truck No. 16738 driven by Peng Taoyuan (28 years old, from Nantong) heading north from the south in the same direction as the tram. For unknown reasons, the truck collided with the tram, and Dai was crushed in the middle, resulting in injuries. The French police of Xiaodongmen sent Dai to Guangci Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective. He died at 10:15 AM yesterday. The police transported the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch for examination. The French authorities were notified to send personnel for inspection today. The deceased's family is still in his hometown, and only a cousin is in Shanghai. The family has been notified.

The Author's Bookstore on Fuzhou Road in this city specializes in accepting consignment sales of exquisite works by national government agencies, academic groups, and individuals, and actively promotes them. It also publishes and distributes a complete catalog of new national publications each month, as a supplement to the consignment book catalog. Over time, this will become a complete national publication catalog. Each book listed in the catalog is extensively described to provide readers with a clearer understanding. Because the catalog meets the psychological needs of readers, it is in high demand, with a monthly distribution of up to 150,000 copies. Those requesting by mail only need to attach five cents for postage. The advertisements on the front page of this newspaper today only represent a portion of the latest publications sold by the bookstore. Furthermore, to facilitate readers in other areas, the bookstore has established a mail-order department. Readers in other areas can entrust the Bank of Communications or the Jin Cheng Bank in their respective regions to collect payments for books, waiving remittance fees. Regardless of whether they purchase books consigned by the bookstore or entrust the bookstore to purchase books from various publishers, all postage for mailing books is waived, and a corresponding discount is provided, so the book price is at least the same as the selling price at the original publishing house. A preferential charter for long-term customers is also available for distribution.

The Situation of the First Literacy Schools in Shanghai (4) 153

— Wu Tiecheng

4. Private Schools and Service Corps

Private literacy schools include the following three types: 1. Those supervised by the Municipal Party Department; 2. Those run by factories, companies, and stores; 3. Those run by individuals. (1) Those supervised by the Municipal Party Department refer to the guidance of various district branches and social and cultural organizations. In total, there are 500 to 600 schools, mostly with one class per school, and only run for one term. Around the end of August, personnel designated by the Party Department supervised the examination using the association's test word list and issued certificates of achievement. The procedures are the same as those of the association. After completion, the results are compiled and sent to the association. (2) Those run by factories, companies, and stores are the labor literacy schools run by factories, companies, and stores jointly supervised by the association and the Social Affairs Bureau. Factories were initially required to report on their labor literacy surveys by the end of July, but to take into account the actual situation, the deadline has been extended to the end of September. These labor literacy schools were originally required to open by August 31, but due to special circumstances, many were unable to do so as scheduled. Currently, 152 schools have already been opened in the city, and it is estimated that no fewer than 300 are being prepared or have been operating but have not yet reported. Guidance and supervision are being provided to each of them. (3) There have also been many cases of individuals with enthusiasm for literacy education who voluntarily requested to run schools. These have been instructed to report to the association through the local district offices for assistance. The literacy education service corps uses students from various elementary schools to teach. Since its implementation, the results have been minimal due to the holidays and the lack of knowledge and preparation of the teachers. Many schools have established private literacy schools to complete their tasks due to the lack of enthusiasm and ability of the students to teach. Further promotion of the service corps requires collective thinking and in-depth research.

Malarial Season 156

— Shijiu

During the summer, malaria is prevalent, so this period is called the "malarial season." This disease is caused by the bite of a mosquito—namely, the female Anopheles mosquito—and has only been confirmed for a little over fifty years. Previously, everyone regarded this disease as a miasma, believing that it was transmitted from polluted air; this disease was especially likely to occur in marshes and other places.

The first person to prove that the female Anopheles mosquito is harmful to humans was Major Laveran, a French military doctor, in 1880. That year, while serving in North Africa, he often found parasites in the blood of malaria patients with the aid of a microscope. In 1898, Sir Ronald Ross, a British military doctor with the rank of major, also found the same parasites in the body of the female Anopheles mosquito in India. These two majors are our benefactors and are forever worthy of commemoration.

Now that malaria had been preliminarily proven to be caused by the female Anopheles mosquito, scientists came forward to conduct further field experiments. In the east of the Tiber River in Italy, there is a large plain that was once regarded as a terrible malarial area. During the malarial season, two scientists went to that place and stayed with the patients. They built a house, opened mesh screens, and lived in it at night. During the day, they naturally came into contact with the patients and even bathed by the river. At night, they allowed the air from the marsh to enter the screen. In this way, although people suffering from malaria surrounded them every day, the two scientists remained healthy. This is an example that proves that to avoid malaria, one must avoid being bitten by the female Anopheles mosquito.

Two doctors from London, England, also volunteered to be bitten by the malarial mosquito. These mosquitoes had bitten patients in Italy and were transported to London in small wooden boxes. After being bitten, the two doctors developed malaria after eighteen days. Parasites were also found in their blood. The doctors who treated them were all unharmed, proving that malaria is not transmitted through the air.

Now the terrible "malarial season" has arrived, so quickly find a way to eliminate those mosquitoes, especially when you see that kind of mosquito perching with its two hind legs high up and its body upright: that is the malarial mosquito!

A Brief Biography of the Person Living Above the Street 157

— Yizhen

The Person Living Above the Street is a pen name; he is actually an unknown writer and an unemployed person who relies on稿費from a few tabloids each month to maintain his livelihood. However, he is also a "romanticist," and his consumption of wine and tobacco is very heavy, so he is hungry for four days out of every ten. Although life is difficult, romance cannot be avoided. He has been in love with a waitress and the landlady's maid, and now he is having a passionate affair with the landlady's sister-in-law. It is said that the landlady's mother is the sister-in-law's mother, but the sister-in-law's father is not the landlady's father. Recently, he gave his lover a piece of cloth, a bottle of perfume, and a bunch of flower threads, with the inscription "I will keep a piece of cloth, a bottle of perfume, and a bunch of flower threads for myself."

His pen name is "The Person Living Above the Street," but he sometimes uses names such as Yingzhen Xiuhua to replace it. Therefore, in addition to letters addressed to Mr. Gu ××, there are also letters addressed to Ms. Gu Xiu× or Gu ×zhen sent to him.

He once invented the "men's breasts are as useless as rat's whiskers" theory, which was admired by his housemate. Someone asked him how he compared himself to men's breasts and rat's whiskers? But he was speechless.

A Figure Who Rises in Society! 158

A Study of the Columns in Front of Barber Shops in Our Country 159

— Yongcai

Regarding the origin of the columns in front of barber shops, in Western countries, it may indeed have originated during the Franco-Prussian War, as Mr. Gu and others stated. However, in our country, there is actually another anecdote-like episode involved. I will record it in this publication without fear of triviality for discussion.

When Emperor Taizu Zhu Hongwu of the Ming Dynasty initially pacified the country and established the capital in Jiangning, because the people's sentiments in various places were turbulent and had not yet been subdued, he was deeply suspicious. After ascending the throne, he ordered a certain general to巡狩in rotation, using this to镇慑. In the general's幕中, there was someone skilled in reading氣 who secretly informed him that the royal氣in Jurong County was very strong and that a覇主would emerge. The general was greatly shocked and immediately drafted a memorial to report it and sought a method of禳解. As a result, a policy of愚民 was implemented!. Jurong residents were forbidden from studying and were not allowed to participate in the imperial examinations. As a result, the talents of Jurong were buried throughout the Ming Dynasty, and none became prominent. However, at that time, the residents of Jurong were very resentful because their prospects for官场had been cut off for no reason. Officials were afraid of inciting incidents and hurriedly reported it. In order to消弭 the怨忿of the Jurong people, Emperor Taizu issued an edict specially allowing the Jurong people to specialize in the barber,修脚, and bamboo industries, and allowing the barber industry to erect旗杆in front of their shops to show glory. Therefore, in front of all barber shops opened by Jurong people, there stood majestic旗杆containing glory. Now, although the旗杆has disappeared due to repeated changes in dynasties. But the columns at the entrance are still a shadow that has been蜕化from the旗杆.

It is said that! On the barber担in Beiping, there is still a旗杆式木杆standing beside the washbasin, which is clear evidence. Moreover, the专营of Jurong people in the barber industry still has this风气, which is also a solid fact.

The Scent of the Imperial Court 160

— Original by Princess Der Ling, translated by Qin Shouou

"But I've been here for a few days, and I haven't seen the bathroom," I asked her.

"What? What are you talking about?" The female official seemed very surprised and asked me back, "Bathroom! What is a bathroom! I really don't understand what you're saying!"

I originally wanted to ask her for instructions, but now she was asking me for instructions. So I tried my best to explain to her what a bathroom meant, but she still didn't quite understand because people at that time didn't investigate these things at all. To wash up, all you needed was a wooden basin. There was no need to open a separate bathroom, so it was naturally difficult for her to understand.

"Since there are no bathroom facilities here, then," I thought to myself, my sister and I were forced to use a wooden basin. The Empress Dowager is such a noble person and has lived in the palace for so long. How could she not have a bathroom? So I couldn't help but ask, "How does the Old Buddha wash?"

"If you want to ask about this, you should just go and see for yourself!" The female official seemed very impatient to talk to me and immediately retorted, "You'll have to go in and serve in a little while anyway. What's the point of being so anxious now? …You don't have to worry about it anyway…!"

I was interrupted by her like this and didn't want to ask any more questions, so I waited patiently with this doubt.

Every time after dinner, the Empress Dowager would always gather us close attendants to sit in her 便殿and chat casually—of course, she was always the one who spoke, and we all listened quietly. What was discussed was nothing more than the various events that had occurred that day or the character of the various ministers inside and outside the palace; it always took about an hour or so before she would retire to her bedroom, and only then could others disperse. (432)

World Oddities

Overseas Anecdotes 161

— Jiyun

The black tide of unemployment has spread to every corner of the world. The Reserve Bank of India in Calcutta recently recruited eighty temporary employees, and more than 10,000 people have volunteered. Before the start of the interview, more than 10,000 people gathered outside the bank gate, cutting off traffic, and the Reserve Bank was forced to temporarily close its business. If each person took one minute for the interview, it would take at least seven days and nights to talk to the volunteers. Because it hindered business, the bank had to announce an indefinite postponement. As a result, the unemployed rioted and later resorted to violence, calling out cavalry and troops to disperse the crowd before business could begin, but the losses were substantial.

In Serbia, an old man named Velimir was originally a very funny optimist. Three years ago, after suddenly crying on the night of the Christmas Eve, he slept all day long. Except for people giving him food to eat, he was permanently asleep. Last October, King Alexander was assassinated. When the old man was eating, his family told him about the king's death. Who knew that after hearing this, his crying illness复发, and he walked to the king's tomb while crying, crying for four days and twelve hours, and then went home and immediately slept. After waking up this time, his actions were normal, and he was still an optimist. Even famous doctors cannot answer the cause of this disease.

In movies, you often see two people fighting, with one person holding a stool and hitting the other on the head, and the stool leg breaks. If the stool were the same as ordinary ones, then the person being hit would at least be seriously injured, if not killed. In fact, the wood of this type of stool is called "Balsa," which is a kind of softwood. One cubic foot weighs only three pounds, and the wood is so soft that it can be broken with teeth, so hitting it on the head will absolutely not cause injury. The wood is produced in the low-lying areas of South America. Since it has been needed in movies, its value has suddenly increased.

Recently, an advertisement with a whimsical idea was found in the American Times: a newly opened "Daily Dog Walking Company." It started with Qimi Taili, who was the supervisor of an apartment building. Women who lived in the apartment often asked him to take their dogs out for a walk with him. Every morning and evening, he became the guardian of the dog walking. Therefore, he suddenly had the idea of opening this unprecedented new company. The rules were: one walk per day, 5 yuan per month; two walks per day, 8 yuan; three walks, 12 yuan; the guardian rests on Sundays. After the company was founded, business was booming, beyond expectations. Many assistants were hired to accompany other people's dogs out for a walk, and now there are more than 10,000 dogs.

On March 25th this year, a vintage auction was held in Paris, France, and one of the items for sale was the original manuscript of the Treaty of Versailles. The manuscript was the achievement of the end of the European War, and although it was only fifteen years ago, it had historical value, so its value was raised to 45,000 francs. The original manuscript was stored by Foreign Minister Bierce, who was assassinated last winter, and many signatures of famous generals were found on his bookshelf.

George Parke Lyttleton, a 49-year-old commercial artist and product decorator from Chicago, USA, recently went to Dr. Frank's hospital in the area to treat a strange disease. Several years ago, he developed an inexplicable disease, and his body gradually turned into that of a monkey. He had large palms, thin wrists, a bent back, and bent feet. Also, his buttocks hurt, and soon a tail grew out. After Dr. Frank's diagnosis, it was said to be related to abnormal secretions of the mucus glands and thyroid gland. It is not yet certain whether he can be restored to being a human.

There are not many types of Japanese surnames, and they also like to use Dalang, Erlang, and Sanlang for names, so there are many people with the same name and surname. The strangest thing is Isohama Town in Ibaraki Prefecture. There are 420 households with the surname "Sekine," accounting for one-quarter of the total. There are very many people with the same name and surname, and there are four or five people with the same name. The postman there, no matter how good your memory is, you are powerless. Therefore, the local postal office notified the residents that any children born in the future must not have the same name as anyone in the 420 households, in order to avoid confusion. But it is also an unprecedented奇事for the authorities to prescribe people's surnames.

Little Western Paradise 162

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty: Struggling to Live to See Her Beloved Grandchild, Bursting into Tears; Remembering the Past in a Year of Famine, Sowing Wheat Brings Disaster

Not only did he know to drink directly from the water, but he also raised a hand, extending a bent finger, pointing towards the back door of Little Western Paradise. No need to guess, it was clear his intention was to see his granddaughter inside, at least his will was very clear. Given the circumstances, it was unlikely he would make false accusations, so he slowly walked closer, his hands behind his back, gazing at them from afar. Suddenly, Hu's sister-in-law raised her head and, seeing someone watching, was startled. She said, "Someone's coming out." The old lady nodded twice in response, her withered hand still trembling, pointing in this direction. Li Shilian thought, "Are they trying to blackmail me?" This thought made his face turn red and then pale, and his heart began to race. From afar, he saw the old lady's lips moving slightly, as if she were saying something. Hu's sister-in-law looked at Li Shilian, then said to the old lady, "This is Old Master Li, not Old Master Jia. He is a friend of Old Master Jia." The old lady then opened her deeply sunken eyes wide, looking at Shilian. It goes without saying, she still held strong hopes for the people inside the back door. Hu's sister-in-law then left him and came forward, saying with a bitter smile, "Old Master Li, look, our relative really misses her granddaughter terribly. Even if she can't come back, just letting my niece stand at the back door for a moment would be enough. You are good friends with Old Master Jia, if you would be willing to speak on our behalf, perhaps it could be done." (335)

Sports News

Participating in the National Games: City Delegation Held Pep Rally Yesterday, Mayor Wu Presented the Flag and Director Pan Gave Instructions, All Athletes Took an Oath Led by Hao Chunde 163

The city's delegation participating in the National Games held a swearing-in and flag presentation ceremony at the City Hall Auditorium at 2:00 PM yesterday. Mayor Wu personally presented the flag and gave instructions, and Director Pan delivered a speech. The ceremony was quite grand. The city's delegation is scheduled to arrive at the venue on the morning of the ninth. Details are as follows:

Full Participation: All staff and athletes of the city's delegation gathered at the YMCA at 1:00 PM yesterday. Cars dispatched by the Education Bureau transported them to the City Hall. In attendance were General Representative Jiang Jianbai, General Leader Shao Rugan, General Secretary Wang Keyong, and over two hundred coaches, managers, and athletes. The Public Security Bureau band played music at the venue. Hu Zongfan, Ding Shoutang, Yuan Zengyu, Shi Weicong, Wu Renya, Yang Zheng, and others served as hosts. The ceremony was performed as scheduled. First, Mayor Wu delivered instructions.

Director's Instructions: Following this, Director Pan of the Municipal Education Bureau delivered a speech, saying, "Everyone, the city has dispatched 233 athletes and 38 staff members, totaling over 270 people, to participate in this National Games. This accounts for about one-tenth of the total number of representatives from all participating units in this National Games, making our delegation larger than most. The Mayor has already given many instructions. I will contribute the four words 'cooperation and advancement' to everyone."

Flag Presentation Ceremony: The Mayor then personally presented the flag, which was received by General Representative Jiang Jianbai. The flag was made of yellow silk, adorned with the words "Sixth National Games Shanghai Municipal Delegation," and had a white pole with red tassels at the top, making it quite bright and eye-catching.

Athlete Oath: After the flag presentation, athlete representative Hao Chunde led everyone in raising their right hands and reading the oath as follows: "Respectfully adhering to the spirit of physical education promoted by the Premier, and as amateur athletes, having been selected as Shanghai Municipal athletes, we are willing to participate in the Sixth National Games, and faithfully abide by the following articles of faith: (1) Obey the command of the General Representative, General Leader, and coaching staff of the city's delegation; (2) Comply with all regulations of the National Games; (3) Adhere to all public order; (4) Obey any refereeing decisions of the National Games referees; (5) Promote the spirit of sportsmanship and chivalry among athletes. We solemnly swear, Athlete So-and-so of Shanghai Municipality." After the oath, slogans were shouted, and photographs were taken before dispersing.

The Tibet Delegation Arriving in Shanghai Yesterday (Wang Kai Photograph)

Naval Personnel from the Weihaiwei District 168

Weihaiwei originally had twenty athletes participating in the National Games, but due to funding issues, the men's basketball team could not participate. The remaining staff, including Bao Nüde, tennis singles Liang Xiaqi, track and field Liu Chongde, Wang Fuhai, Cao Yanyou, pentathlon Yuan Xingwen, and swimming Liu Zenghou, a total of seven people, led by General Leader Gu Tuier, set off on the fifth of this month and arrived in Shanghai at 1:30 PM yesterday. At around 2:00 PM, they reported to the organizing committee. According to General Leader Gu, due to economic constraints in Weihaiwei, the already registered men's basketball team could not participate, which is deeply regrettable. Furthermore, the people there do not pay much attention to sports, as popular education has not yet been universal. Last year, there were three junior high schools in the entire district, one of which was a church school, but due to a lack of funding, it was closed this spring. Therefore, only two junior high schools remain, and the schools do not focus on physical education. Consequently, most of the athletes participating this time are naval personnel. Women's sports are even more backward, so no women are participating this time. The purpose of this team's participation in the National Games is not to win medals. Being able to gather with athletes from all over the country in one place will at least provide many benefits.

Seventeen Athletes from Tibet 169

The Tibet delegation participating in the National Games consists of seventeen people, led by General Leader Huang Cishu. They arrived in Shanghai from Beijing yesterday and immediately reported to the organizing committee. According to Mr. Huang, the province is located in the remote northwest, and its culture is underdeveloped. Most of the athletes participating this time are from Tibetan schools. Their purpose is only to observe and learn from others, so that people across the country can recognize the Tibetan flag and pay attention to it. The list is as follows: Leader Huang Cishu, Manager Wang Ke'an, Athletes Li Renhuo, Cai Rang, Jiang Zuo, Bao Xingchang, Dan Ba, Long Ben, Zhan Leqing, Qin Youyi, Ren Bandan, Shi Maozhou, Wang Xu, Zhou Ben, Ma Xingrong, Kui Xuan, and others, a total of seventeen people, participating in basketball, volleyball, and track and field.

Athletes from Shaanxi Come from Afar 170

Shaanxi has paid great attention to sports in the past four years. In addition to setting up physical education courses in various schools, the Party, government, military, and school sports promotion association was organized this summer to encourage all citizens to pay attention to sports. Most of the athletes participating in the National Games this time are from various schools. They set off on the fourth of this month, led by General Leader Zhang Ziyao, and arrived in Shanghai by express train at 7:15 AM on the seventh. Many fellow villagers from various teams went to the port to welcome them. Jiangsu, Anhui, Suiyuan, and Others Arrived in Shanghai Last Night 172

A group of ninety-six Jiangsu athletes and staff members, departing from six districts, arrived at the North Station for assembly at 6:30 PM yesterday. Twenty-four male and female athletes from Anhui Province, led by General Leader Luo Liangzhu, arrived in Shanghai on the same train as the Jiangsu athletes at 6:30 PM yesterday. All Jiangsu Athletes Arrived in Shanghai 173

A total of ninety-four male and female athletes and twenty staff members from Jiangsu Province attending the National Games, led by General Leader Zhang Dongping, arrived in Shanghai. Athletes from the fourth district arrived on the Shanghai-Hangzhou train, and athletes from the fifth district arrived on the Dada Wheel, one after another in the morning and afternoon yesterday. Athletes from the first, second, third, seventh, and eighth districts arrived by ordinary express train from Beijing at 9:30 AM yesterday morning. They assembled along the way and arrived in Shanghai completely at 6:40 PM in the afternoon. The organizing committee immediately dispatched several large cars to the venue for lodging. As long as it was not past the office hours of the organizing committee, they were scheduled to report to the organizing committee that day.

Before and After Departure

The Jiangsu athletes were assembled in advance by the Provincial Games Committee in seven locations: Xuzhou, Nanjing, Zhenjiang, Wuxi, Suzhou, Songjiang, and Nantong. Those in Nantong took the Dada Wheel and arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning, first going to the athlete dormitory at the National Games venue to rest. The athletes from the fifth district took the Shanghai-Hangzhou train from Songjiang and arrived in Shanghai at around 4:00 PM, waiting at the station for the large team to assemble. Eighteen male and female athletes from the eighth district, led by Wu Yihong and Qin Weiming, arrived in Beijing on the evening of the sixth. Together with General Leader Zhang Dongping and staff members Xu Xiaochuan and Yuan Jidong, who were in Beijing, they departed from Beijing at 9:30 AM yesterday morning. The railway added more than ten athletes and staff members from the first district. More than twenty people were added in Wuxi, and more than twenty people were added in Suzhou. Except for a few athletes who arrived in Shanghai on their own, the rest arrived in Shanghai with the large team. Short-distance famous athlete Cheng Jinguan was slightly unwell yesterday and is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on his own today.

A Glimpse of Strength

The strength of the Jiangsu Province athletes in this National Games is average, with track and field being relatively better. Cheng Jinguan's short-distance running and middle hurdles, Zeng Rongzhong and Li Yanxiang's middle-distance running, and Jin Zhongkang's long-distance running all have hopes of scoring points in the National Games. In women's track and field, Pang Sao Wang's short-distance running and two jumps, and Wu Juxin's short-distance running are the most promising. Yuan Yuanshi's long jump once reached 4.89 meters, breaking the national record, and her high jump also reached 1.30 meters, so scoring points should not be a problem. If they work hard, their names should appear on the list for the two short-distance runners. Ball sports are not in good shape. Men's volleyball and soccer were not selected. The strength of the basketball team is still acceptable. Apart from strong enemies such as Beijing, Shanghai, Pingjin, and Wuhan, Jiangsu can be counted among the top teams. Women's basketball and volleyball are better and may advance to the semi-finals.

Beijing Athletes Arrived in Shanghai This Morning 174

(Nanjing, 7th Dispatch) All athletes of the Beijing National Games delegation held a swearing-in ceremony at the Beijing Municipal Government Auditorium at 2:00 PM on the 7th. Mayor Ma presided over the oath and delivered instructions, stating that the delegation has a heavy responsibility, hoping that they would pay attention to sportsmanship and sports ethics, while complying with the order of the conference and obeying discipline. In an environment of caution and vigilance, they should strive unceasingly to achieve success, and hoping that the delegation's actions would serve as a model for the National Games and establish a good reputation. After the speech, Mayor Ma personally presented the flag, and General Leader Chen Jianru attended to receive it. Finally, athlete representative Chen Qing delivered a response. The entire delegation is scheduled to go to Shanghai led by Chen Jianru on the morning of the 8th to join forces.

The Sixth National Games is scheduled to open on October 10th at the Shanghai Stadium in the city center. Over a thousand representatives from various organizations attended, and the atmosphere was very enthusiastic. Details are recorded as follows:

Participating Organizations

In attendance were Hu Wenhu, Lin Jindian, Wang Jingcheng, Lin Aimin, and all the Malayan Chinese athletes, as well as Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Education Bureau Director Pan Gongzhan, Social Affairs Bureau Director Wu Xingya (represented by Zhang Hui), Health Bureau Director Li Ting'an, Public Security Bureau Director Cai Jingjun, Xu Shiying from the various provinces' flood relief associations, Yang Hu from the Security Office, Du Yuesheng from the Municipal Council, Li Dachao from the Aviation Association, Yu Zuoting from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Yang Weiyu from the Vocational Education Society, Wu Deyin from the World Student Association, He Bingsong from Jinan University, Liu Haisu from the Shanghai Academy of Fine Arts, Hu Duanxing from Jiaotong University, Ye Zhendong from the Shanghai County Government, Pei Shunyuan from the Xinwenbao, Shen Songfang, Hu Zongfan from the Chenbao, Teng Shugu from the Shibao, Chen Dongbai and Zhu Zhiming from the Shanghai News Agency, Sun Mingqi from the Shangbao, Ruan Weicun from the Qinfen Daily, Wang Xiaoying from the China Women's High School, Gu Jingji from Chongjing Middle School, Hu Xiyuan from the Industrial Federation, Yuan Zengyu from the Municipal Sports Association, Yan Fuqing from the Anti-Tuberculosis Association, and representatives from ninety-seven other organizations, totaling over a thousand people.

Welcome Scene

The meeting commenced at 3:00 PM, with Pan Gongzhan, Wu Xingya, Du Yuesheng, Xu Shiying, Yang Xiaotian, Li Dachao, Yu Zuoting, and others serving as members of the presidium, Hu Guigeng as the master of ceremonies, and Zheng Jie, Chen Baohua, Nie Haifan, Chen Shuo, and others as greeters. After the formalities, Presidium member Xu Shiying delivered a welcome speech. Mayor Wu and Director Pan gave speeches. Subsequently, Hu Wenhu, the general team leader of the Malayan team, delivered a response. Finally, refreshments were served, and entertainment was provided. The meeting concluded around 6:00 PM.

Chairman's Address

Presidium member Xu Shiying delivered a welcome speech, saying, "The Sixth National Games is being held at the city center sports ground. Over one hundred and fifty people, led by General Team Leader Mr. Hu Wenhu, Deputy Team Leader Mr. Lin Jindian, and Mr. Wang Jingcheng, have returned to the country, pioneering the participation of overseas Chinese in the grand gathering of the motherland. This is truly a magnificent undertaking. Mr. Hu, Mr. Lin, and Mr. Wang are not only leaders of the overseas Chinese but also care about the motherland and are particularly enthusiastic about social welfare and charitable causes, which have long been admired by the people of the country. This time, leading young overseas Chinese back from afar to participate in the National Games and tour the motherland will allow them to gain a deep impression of the motherland's politics and construction. The significance of this is profound and manifold. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, local associations, the China Aviation Association, and ninety-seven other organizations are holding a welcome rally today at the Greater Shanghai Garden. I would like to wish all leaders and athletes good health and a bright future. I offer these humble words to express my admiration and to commemorate this unforgettable occasion."

Key Points of Speeches

Subsequently, Director Pan of the Municipal Education Bureau delivered a speech, roughly stating that the Shanghai community's welcome rally for the Malayan Chinese athletes is unprecedented in Shanghai and rare even in China. Our country has held National Games more than once, and even since the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, it has been held three times, but overseas Chinese have never participated. This time, Mr. Hu Wenhu and others led athletes from Malaya back to participate, which is truly an unprecedented grand event. The people of the country should welcome them to commemorate this occasion. However, today's welcome is different from ordinary social events. The significance is briefly described as follows: Shanghai is a place of international observation, and this National Games is being held in Shanghai. During this Games, we can demonstrate the spirit of unity of the entire country, and especially the power of deep cooperation between overseas Chinese and the motherland. If this National Games lacked the participation of overseas Chinese, its significance would be greatly reduced, and the interest would definitely not be as strong. The National Games treats all units equally, but the reason why the Shanghai community especially welcomes the overseas Chinese athletes is because Dr. Sun Yat-sen received the greatest help from the overseas Chinese in the revolution. Therefore, today we have the opportunity to witness the participation of overseas Chinese who have helped the revolution the most in the grand event of the National Games, and the people of the country should sincerely welcome them. As for Mr. Hu Wenhu, the general team leader of your team, who is eager for public good and is known for his benevolence, he is now promoting sports with all his might, which deserves special admiration, which goes without saying, and so on. Next, Mayor Wu gave a speech.

Mr. Hu's Reply

The general team leader of the Malayan athletes, Hu Wenhu, delivered a reply, saying, "This time, we are participating in the National Games, and it is a great honor and gratitude to receive such a grand reception today by representatives of various organizations. The first significance of this trip is to promote sports and learn from each other, so that the athletes can return to Southeast Asia and make further efforts. Secondly, the athletes are very unfamiliar with the situation in the motherland. After returning to the country this time, they will also need to sightsee after participating in the National Games to gain a deep impression and enhance the patriotic thinking of the overseas Chinese. As for the various instructions given to us today by the chairman, the mayor, and Director Pan, we will certainly never forget them," and so on.

Refreshments and Entertainment

The final refreshments and entertainment program are as follows: 1. English song by Ms. Lang Yuxiu; 2. Kunqu opera by Ms. Wang Jie; 3. Song by Ms. Li Lili; 4. "Jasmine Nostalgia" by Ms. Bai Hong; 5. New Moon Dance by Ms. Li Mingjian and members of the New Moon Society's dance troupe; 6. Harmonica performance by the China Harmonica Association; 7. Song and dance by Xingzhong Elementary School; 8. Chinese martial arts by the Jingwu Athletic Association. Ms. Hu Die was originally scheduled to sing yesterday, but she was unable to perform as she did not bring her musical instruments. She only stood up and delivered a simple welcome speech.

Parade Today

Various organizations in the city will host a car parade throughout the city for the Malayan Chinese athletes, which is scheduled to take place at 1:00 PM today. In addition to the cars provided by the organizations themselves, the remaining cars will be provided by the Xiang Sheng Car Company in Shanghai. The route was determined by the preparatory meeting as follows: The athletes' cars will depart from Liangjiang, and the cars of the hosting organizations will depart from the YMCA at Baxianqiao. They will pass through Wenmiao Road in the South City, enter Zhizaoju Road, visit the Jiangnan Shipyard and the Naval Aircraft Factory, return north through Zhejiang Road, pass through Nanjing Road, head east to the Outer Baibo Bridge, turn into North Suzhou Road, pass through North Sichuan Road and Bazilu Road, enter Baoshan Road, pass through Tiantong'an Road, and arrive at the city center to visit the municipal government's construction projects. Then they will enter Jungong Road, pass through Yunzaobang, arrive at Wusong, visit the fort, and return to Shanghai around 6:00 PM.

Mr. Ma's Banquet

Mr. Hu recently took advantage of Chairman Lin's visit to Shanghai to pay a visit to the chairman's private residence on Rue Cardinal Mercier with several important members of the Malayan Chinese team and reported on the situation of the overseas Chinese. Tomorrow afternoon, the ninety-seven-year-old Ma Ganbo will host a banquet at the Tushanwan Catholic Church. In the afternoon at 3:00 PM, the Guangdong Fellow Villagers Association will host a tea party at the New Asia Restaurant to welcome General Team Leader Hu and all the staff and athletes to express their appreciation. It is heard that various circles admire Mr. Hu's spirit of caring for the motherland and promoting sports, as he led the Malayan Chinese athletes to return to the country for the first time to participate in the National Games and assumed all the expenses of the team. After the closing ceremony of the National Games, Mr. Hu will travel to Beijing and then to Sichuan, Guizhou, and Yunnan to conduct inspections in order to seek investment and development in our country's industries.

Hubei Football Team Defeats Shanghai Guangdong - Ten to Zero - 181

The Hubei football team, which is participating in the National Games, arrived in Shanghai on the 5th. Many of the team's players are also well-known figures. The forwards are sharp, so the team's strength is quite strong. They defeated the Shanghai Guangdong team by a large margin of ten to zero. A brief record of the battle is as follows:

First Half Seven to Zero Yin Jiao Mingming, the beginning touched, Jiang Chao commanded the three armies, and led the troops south. Hu Ke'an intercepted it at the border, and Deng Ziyang kicked it in, opening the scoring. Jiang Chao and Fu Zhibin were unwilling to be left behind, and each scored a goal. The Shanghai Guangdong team resisted bravely, but the forwards were weak and could not attack repeatedly. Hubei's offense was very good, and Deng Ziyang, Fu Zhibin, and Jiang Chao made another contribution, resulting in a score of seven to zero at the end of the first half.

Second Half Two to Zero The Shanghai Guangdong team made major adjustments to their lineup, thinking about revenge. The entire team of soldiers charged with all their might, winning three penalty kicks, but their feet were weak, their shots were inaccurate, and they still gained nothing. Jiang Chao waved his troops again, penetrating deep into the hinterland, and Fu Zhibin and Peng Kangqi made another contribution. Zhu Yunlong, sitting in the center back, saw that the forwards had made their own contributions, and his ambition was soaring. He shot remotely at the goal from thirty yards, hitting the center of the river, making it ten. The lineup is recorded below:

Simple Rules for Supplying Photos of the National Games 187

Price List for Ordering Negatives Announced

The simple rules for supplying photos of the National Games are announced as follows:

(1) These simple rules are formulated in accordance with Article 7 of the Journalist Registration Regulations established by this committee.

(2) In order to take photos without omissions and to provide systematic news photos, this committee has specially appointed a photography studio to undertake the official photography duties of the conference, which will be supervised and guided by the publicity team of this committee.

(3) Any photos that have not been reviewed and approved by the Publicity Team shall not be distributed or sold by the photography studio undertaking the work; violations will be subject to appropriate penalties, or the right to undertake the photography of the conference will be revoked.

(4) Guests, spectators, and journalists of the conference who need a full set of photos can pre-order or temporarily order from the photography studio undertaking the photography of the conference. The price is fifteen silver dollars.

(5) Those who make the above pre-order must specify in advance whether the pre-ordered photos need to be delivered by personnel sent by the photography studio undertaking the work for this committee, or whether they will pick them up in person at the committee, or whether they will be delivered by the post office. The photography studio undertaking the work must distribute them at 3:00 PM, 6:00 PM, and 8:00 PM every day according to the needs of each subscriber.

(6) Sample prints of news photos will be displayed in the journalists' lounge and the conference photo exhibition area for journalists and spectators to choose from.

(7) Guests, spectators, and journalists of the conference who need to select and purchase designated photos and need to pick them up within three hours will be priced as follows: 4-inch, 30 cents silver dollar; 6-inch, 50 cents silver dollar; 8-inch, 70 cents silver dollar; 12-inch, one silver dollar; prices for sizes larger than 12-inch are negotiable.

(8) Guests, spectators, and journalists of the conference who need to select and purchase designated photos and pick them up the next day will be priced as follows: 4-inch, 15 cents silver dollar; 6-inch, 15 cents silver dollar; 8-inch, 40 cents silver dollar; 12-inch, 70 cents silver dollar; prices for sizes larger than 11-inch are negotiable.

(9) The photography studio undertaking the work must charge according to the prices set in these simple rules and must not raise prices; it must deliver the goods within the time specified in these simple rules and must not be overdue.

Correction of the Usage of Badges and Certificates 191

In the first article of the Regulations on the Use of Badges and Certificates of the 6th National Games published yesterday, "Preparatory Committee members, competition committee members, and referees all wear 'large red badges with golden tassels of nine characters,'" there is an error; it should be "red badges." Also, in the eighth article, "Visiting the competition," should be changed to "Gymnasiums, swimming pools, and baseball stadium stands, except for special seats, can also be freely entered and visited. However, the tennis court and volleyball court require purchasing tickets for seating, except for referees of each item." This correction is hereby made.

Fudan University Holds Grand Celebration for 30th Anniversary 194

Honorary Degrees Awarded to Sun Ke and Others, Exhibition of Achievements by All Deans

—World Newspaper Exhibition Held Simultaneously—

Private Fudan University in this city has a history of thirty years since its founding. In order to commemorate its 30th anniversary, the university held a grand commemorative meeting at its campus in Jiangwan, and also performed military chemistry demonstrations, exhibitions of achievements of various departments, a world newspaper exhibition, a biology exhibition, and a domestic industrial products exhibition. A ceremony for awarding honorary degrees was also held. The details are listed below:

List of Participants

Sun Ke, Wang Zhengting, Zhao Jinqing, Cheng Tianfang, Li Zhaohuan, Liu Zhanen, Zhang Yong, Ou Chuai, Luo Yunyan, Zhu Shaoping, Jiang Yiping, Jin Jianyuan, Yin Zhangrui, Han Qiaqing, Bing Xueqiao, and the university's president Li Denghui, deans and department heads Gu Zhongyi, Zhang Youer, Xie Liuchuan, and representatives of various institutions, as well as more than 2,000 students. The chairman was Li Denghui. The opening ceremony was held at 4:00 PM. After the formal ceremony, the chairman delivered an opening speech.

Chairman's Speech

Chairman Li Denghui's speech briefly stated that the university has been established for thirty years, and it is a great honor to hold a grand commemorative meeting here today and to have all the guests participate. It should be known that the university's existence today is not easy. I would like to report the history of the university to everyone. The university was founded in the year of Yisi in the Guangxu reign, organized by students who split from Aurora University. At that time, the school site was in Wusong. In the first year of the Republic of China, it was moved to Xujiahui. It was presented to the Nanjing Provisional Government for approval and received 10,000 taels of silver in assistance. In the eleventh year of the Republic of China, it moved to the current campus in Jiangwan. After more than ten years of operation, it has reached today's scale. The university has always upheld the principle of hard work, so it has tried its best to economize on administrative expenses in order to achieve this result, which has been recognized by all sectors of society. The country is in dire need of talent. The future development of the university will depend on the enthusiastic assistance of the countrymen. Then he read the congratulatory telegrams and letters from all walks of life, and then the representative of the board of directors, Wang Zhengting, delivered a speech, the representative of the Beijing Alumni Association delivered a congratulatory speech, the representative of Shanghai universities, Li Zhaohuan, delivered a congratulatory speech, the representative of the alumni association, Cheng Tianfang, delivered a congratulatory speech, and the representative of the professors, Zhang Youer, delivered a congratulatory speech. Then the awarding of honorary degrees began.

Honorary Degrees

A total of twelve people were awarded honorary degrees. Those awarded doctoral degrees were Sun Ke, Cheng Dafang, Guo Yunquan, Jin Wensi, Guo Renyuan, Jiang Yiping. Those awarded master's degrees were Zhu Shaoping, Yin Zhangrui. Those awarded bachelor's degrees were Yang Beihuan, Hong Weixiong, Yang Zicheng, and Leng Xueqiao.

Celebration Held at Xujiahui High School

On the 7th, 8th, and 9th days of this month, Fudan University and Xujiahui High School held a 30th anniversary celebration. In addition to sending a part of the students and extracting a part of the students' works to participate in the performance and exhibition of the university department, a very grand flag raising ceremony was held again at 9:00 AM yesterday. At 7:00 PM in the evening, Yue Ming Film Company donated a domestic film. It is heard that there will be a military parade and achievement exhibition today, and the opening ceremony of Denghui Hall will be held. In the afternoon, there will also be sports ball games, drama flame programs, and other programs. Tomorrow, there will be more exciting scout performances and Yuyi Peking Opera and other programs to mark the celebration.

Welcoming Chen Chongli Back to China 196

Mr. Chen Chongli has served in cotton mills in Wuxi and Wujin, etc., in this city for more than ten years. He is well-versed in both theoretical and practical knowledge. He sees that the Chinese textile industry is on the verge of danger and is eager to make improvements. Therefore, in April of this year, he resolutely went abroad to Japan for investigation. During his half-year stay in Japan, he carefully investigated famous Japanese textile institutions such as the Toa Textile Co., Ltd. Asada Factory, and Meiji Textile Co., Ltd. Yukihashi Factory, etc., and gained a lot. It is recently learned that Mr. Chen is scheduled to return to China before the Double Tenth Festival. Colleagues in the textile industry in this city believe that Mr. Chen's investigation will definitely make a great contribution, and are now preparing to welcome him.

Little Man (69) 197

— Original by American Ms. Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang

"He is the only boy we have ever failed with, and I am really sad. I originally thought he had many faults, but his nature could still enable him to become a good person."

When Tang En heard Mrs. Pei sigh, he himself wanted to ask for another chance, but his arrogance would not allow him to do so. So he walked out, his face still indifferent, but he shook hands silently and left with Mr. Pei, leaving only Nai De and Mrs. Shu to send him off with tears, standing and gazing in disappointment.

A few days later, they received a letter from Mr. Bei, reporting that Tang En was doing well, and they were naturally overjoyed to hear that. But three weeks later, another letter came, saying that Tang En had run away, and there was no news of his whereabouts. They were all worried when they heard that. So Pei Jiusheng said:

"Maybe I should have given him a chance then."

But this time, Mrs. Pei nodded, as if she had great insight, and said, "Don't regret it, don't try to regret it, the child will come back, I am very sure of this."

But as the days went by, Tang En did not even show his shadow.

Qingdao Japanese Yarn Factory Resolves to Reduce Production 203

The Qingdao Japanese Yarn Factory, due to rural poverty and financial stagnation, is seeking to increase yarn prices and implement free production cuts of 70% or 50%. However, the economic panic still shows no signs of recovery. If the yarn factory industry continues to wait and see, it will inevitably lead to overproduction. Increased inventory will only make capital turnover more difficult. Recently, the industry has decided to expand production cuts to 30% through meetings and has requested instructions from the Japan-China Textile Industry Association headquarters in Osaka. After approval, the gradual implementation will begin. The decision to cut production by 30% is still based on the extreme policy of maintaining the current market price in order to overcome the difficulties of the yarn factory industry.
